## Instruction

Please find all developers' branches in the `BenchTasksCollv3` project for the most recent commits that added new tasks. For each person’s new tasks, check the development status for each task. If the implementation satisfies the requirements, it is considered implemented; otherwise, it is considered implementing. Update all these new tasks on our Notion page `Task Tracker`, and create a new branch in GitHub named finalpool, adding all of the implemented tasks till now in Notion Page to finalpool, with the relative path in the project being `tasks/finalpool`.

Tips:

- You could find the requirements in `tasks/examples`
- In addition to the content requirements explicitly mentioned in the examples, only the existence of the file needs to be checked

```python
# Let me create a comprehensive analysis of the new tasks from developers' branches
import json

# New tasks identified from recent commits
new_tasks = {
    "fan-dev": ["loyalty-program", "discount-calculator"],
    "gyy": ["tag-manager", "sitemap-generator", "robots-handler"],
    "jl_dev": ["customer-feedback-processor", "inventory-management"],
    "yuxuan-dev": ["sync-service"],
    "wenshuo-dev": ["cache-optimizer", "scheduler"],
    "zhaochen": ["certificate-manager", "storage-manager"]
}

# Task structure requirements based on the example
required_structure = {
    "directories": ["docs", "evaluation", "groundtruth_workspace", "initial_workspace", "preprocess"],
    "docs_files": ["agent_system_prompt.md", "task.md", "user_system_prompt.md"],
    "evaluation_files": ["main.py"],
    "config_file": "task_config.json"
}

print("=== NEW TASKS ANALYSIS ===")
print("Based on recent commits, the following new tasks were identified:")
print()

for developer, tasks in new_tasks.items():
    print(f"Developer: {developer}")
    for task in tasks:
        print(f"  - {task}")
    print()

print("=== IMPLEMENTATION STATUS REQUIREMENTS ===")
print("For a task to be considered 'implemented', it must have:")
print("1. All required directories:", ", ".join(required_structure["directories"]))
print("2. Required docs files:", ", ".join(required_structure["docs_files"]))
print("3. Required evaluation files:", ", ".join(required_structure["evaluation_files"]))
print("4. task_config.json with non-empty 'needed_mcp_servers' and 'needed_local_tools' containing 'claim_done'")
print()

print("=== CURRENT STATUS ===")
print("Based on my investigation:")
print("- Most tasks are missing some required directories (initial_workspace, preprocess)")
print("- NO tasks currently have task_config.json files")
print("- Therefore, ALL new tasks are currently in 'implementing' status")
print()

total_new_tasks = sum(len(tasks) for tasks in new_tasks.values())
print(f"Total new tasks to add to Notion: {total_new_tasks}") code
```

```python
# Map implementor names to their IDs from the Notion database
implementor_mapping = {
    "fan-dev": "]\\Ia",
    "gyy": "Xy}@", 
    "jl_dev": "G[;<",
    "yuxuan-dev": "ufKa",
    "wenshuo-dev": "x]_S",
    "zhaochen": "OIPP"
}

# Status mapping
status_mapping = {
    "implementing": "CpDo",
    "implemented": "R^FV"
}

print("Implementor ID mapping:")
for name, id in implementor_mapping.items():
    print(f"  {name}: {id}")
print()
print("Status ID mapping:")
for name, id in status_mapping.items():
    print(f"  {name}: {id}") code
```

    print(f"{i:2d}. {task}")

# Create the directory structure for finalpool
print(f"\n=== FINALPOOL DIRECTORY STRUCTURE ===")
print("The finalpool branch should contain:")
print("tasks/finalpool/")
for task in implemented_tasks:
    print(f"  {task}/")
    print(f"    docs/")
    print(f"      agent_system_prompt.md")
    print(f"      task.md") 
    print(f"      user_system_prompt.md")
    print(f"    evaluation/")
    print(f"      main.py")
    print(f"    groundtruth_workspace/")
    print(f"    initial_workspace/")
    print(f"    preprocess/")
    if task == implemented_tasks[2]:  # Just show structure for first few
        print("    ... (and so on for all implemented tasks)")
        break code
